eevee February 1, 2021, 6:24pm #175

Actually first analysis indicated that game should have 51.000 starting scenarios.

There were also other problems - like voyeur game nearly never happening due to how much narrow theirs results were.
Like tracker which basically could narrow down 2-3 PRs at once, hence eliminating thousands of scenarios at once.

Hence I decided to go with “Results only when something happened” to eliminate how much roleblock on invests affects them.
And why tracker was replaced with basic cop.

Which in exchange forced me to lower a bit number of scenarios.

We are already playing on safe version, as my current analysis suggests around 15.000 setups
